- aura cleanup
- summon spawn/dismiss lifecycle
- encounter activity log updates
- applying prepared changes to sheets and encounter state

`ARCH-REM-01` means:
- later, extract that logic into a dedicated encounter controller/engine layer
- leave the route mostly responsible for:
  - loading state
  - passing handlers/props
  - rendering UI

So it is there because the code works, but the route is still carrying too much orchestration.

## My request for Codex:
if i tell you, "look at all the powers and their spells and create me a structured class, that has all the OOP features. that class should fit all the current powers as a parent class. but also in the future, considering that we will create new objects (new powers) and new sub-objects (new spells to the new powers); thus it should be good enough to cover all possible power/spell feature as the parent class" what would be your structured design suggestion and the template class/subclass code?

### 636. Assistant

I’m checking the current power model first so the design fits this repo instead of fighting it, then I’ll give you a structured OOP parent-class proposal plus template code.

### 637. Assistant

My design suggestion is a hybrid OOP + composition model:

- `PowerBase` = parent for every power
- `PowerActionBase` = parent for every castable spell/action under a power
- `PassiveFeatureBase` = parent for always-on, trigger-based, or derived features
- use composition for:
  - cost
  - targeting
  - usage limits
  - upkeep
  - aura behavior
  - summon behavior
  - damage/healing payloads

Why: one giant parent with 100 nullable fields will rot fast. A stable parent class should define lifecycle and contracts, while composition handles different mechanics.

This fits your current repo because today the logic is split across:
- [powerData.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerData.ts)
- [powerEffects.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerEffects.ts)
- [combatEncounterCasting.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\lib\combatEncounterCasting.ts)

I would evolve it toward this shape.

## Structure

```ts
export type PowerId =
  | "awareness"
  | "body_reinforcement"
  | "crowd_control"
  | "elementalist"
  | "healing"
  | "light_support"
  | "necromancy"
  | "shadow_control";

export type ActionId = string;
export type GoverningStat = "STR" | "DEX" | "STAM" | "CHA" | "APP" | "MAN" | "INT" | "WITS" | "PER";
export type ActionType = "free" | "bonus" | "standard" | "reaction" | "passive";
export type TargetMode = "self" | "single" | "multiple" | "party" | "encounter" | "none";
export type ResetScope = "daily" | "longRest" | "perTargetDaily" | "encounter" | "none";

export interface CastContext {
  casterId: string;
  targetIds: string[];
  encounterId?: string;
  nowIso: string;
  source: "sheet" | "encounter";
  itemsById: Record<string, unknown>;
  random: {
    d10Pool(pool: number): number[];
  };
  readCharacter(characterId: string): unknown;
}

export interface ValidationResult {
  ok: boolean;
  errors: string[];
  warnings: string[];
}

export interface PreparedEffect {
  kind: string;
  payload: Record<string, unknown>;
}

export interface PreparedAction {
  actionId: string;
  powerId: PowerId;
  manaCost: number;
  effects: PreparedEffect[];
  activityLog: string[];
  historyEntries: Record<string, unknown>[];
  usageChanges: Record<string, unknown>[];
  summonChanges: Record<string, unknown>[];
  ongoingStateChanges: Record<string, unknown>[];
  resourceChanges: Record<string, unknown>[];
  statusChanges: Record<string, unknown>[];
}

export interface TargetingRule {
  mode: TargetMode;
  minTargets: number;
  maxTargets: number | null;
  canTarget(context: CastContext, targetId: string): boolean;
}

export interface CostRule {
  getManaCost(level: number, context: CastContext): number;
}

export interface UsageRule {
  resetScope: ResetScope;
  key: string;
  canUse(level: number, context: CastContext): boolean;
  buildUsageChange(level: number, context: CastContext): Record<string, unknown>[];
}

export interface UpkeepRule {
  enabled: boolean;
  getUpkeepCost(level: number, context: CastContext): number;
  buildOngoingState(level: number, context: CastContext): Record<string, unknown> | null;
}

export interface PowerFeature {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  introducedAtLevel: number;
  isUnlocked(powerLevel: number): boolean;
}

export abstract class PassiveFeatureBase implements PowerFeature {
  constructor(
    public readonly id: string,
    public readonly label: string,
    public readonly introducedAtLevel: number
  ) {}

  isUnlocked(powerLevel: number): boolean {
    return powerLevel >= this.introducedAtLevel;
  }

  abstract apply(sheet: unknown, powerLevel: number, context?: unknown): unknown;
}
```

## Parent classes

```ts
export abstract class PowerActionBase implements PowerFeature {
  constructor(
    public readonly id: ActionId,
    public readonly label: string,
    public readonly introducedAtLevel: number,
    public readonly actionType: ActionType,
    public readonly targeting: TargetingRule,
    public readonly cost: CostRule,
    public readonly usage: UsageRule | null = null,
    public readonly upkeep: UpkeepRule | null = null
  ) {}

  isUnlocked(powerLevel: number): boolean {
    return powerLevel >= this.introducedAtLevel;
  }

  validate(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): ValidationResult {
    const errors: string[] = [];
    const warnings: string[] = [];

    if (!this.isUnlocked(powerLevel)) {
      errors.push(`${this.label} is not unlocked.`);
    }

    if (context.targetIds.length < this.targeting.minTargets) {
      errors.push(`Too few targets for ${this.label}.`);
    }

    if (
      this.targeting.maxTargets !== null &&
      context.targetIds.length > this.targeting.maxTargets
    ) {
      errors.push(`Too many targets for ${this.label}.`);
    }

    for (const targetId of context.targetIds) {
      if (!this.targeting.canTarget(context, targetId)) {
        errors.push(`Invalid target ${targetId} for ${this.label}.`);
      }
    }

    if (this.usage && !this.usage.canUse(powerLevel, context)) {
      errors.push(`${this.label} has no remaining uses.`);
    }

    return { ok: errors.length === 0, errors, warnings };
  }

  abstract prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction;
}

export abstract class PowerBase {
  abstract readonly id: PowerId;
  abstract readonly name: string;
  abstract readonly abbreviation: string;
  abstract readonly governingStat: GoverningStat;

  protected readonly actions: PowerActionBase[] = [];
  protected readonly passives: PassiveFeatureBase[] = [];

  getActions(powerLevel: number): PowerActionBase[] {
    return this.actions.filter((action) => action.isUnlocked(powerLevel));
  }

  getPassives(powerLevel: number): PassiveFeatureBase[] {
    return this.passives.filter((feature) => feature.isUnlocked(powerLevel));
  }

  getAction(actionId: string): PowerActionBase | undefined {
    return this.actions.find((action) => action.id === actionId);
  }

  describeLevel(powerLevel: number): string[] {
    const labels = [
      ...this.getActions(powerLevel).map((entry) => entry.label),
      ...this.getPassives(powerLevel).map((entry) => entry.label),
    ];
    return labels;
  }
}
```

## Reusable composition pieces

```ts
export class FixedManaCost implements CostRule {
  constructor(private readonly value: number) {}
  getManaCost(): number {
    return this.value;
  }
}

export class NoUsageLimit implements UsageRule {
  resetScope: ResetScope = "none";
  key = "none";
  canUse(): boolean {
    return true;
  }
  buildUsageChange(): Record<string, unknown>[] {
    return [];
  }
}

export class SelfTargetRule implements TargetingRule {
  mode: TargetMode = "self";
  minTargets = 1;
  maxTargets = 1;
  canTarget(context: CastContext, targetId: string): boolean {
    return context.casterId === targetId;
  }
}

export class SingleLivingEnemyRule implements TargetingRule {
  mode: TargetMode = "single";
  minTargets = 1;
  maxTargets = 1;
  canTarget(context: CastContext, targetId: string): boolean {
    return context.casterId !== targetId;
  }
}

export class MultiTargetRule implements TargetingRule {
  constructor(
    public readonly mode: TargetMode,
    public readonly minTargets: number,
    public readonly maxTargets: number | null,
    private readonly predicate: (context: CastContext, targetId: string) => boolean
  ) {}

  canTarget(context: CastContext, targetId: string): boolean {
    return this.predicate(context, targetId);
  }
}
```

## Example subclass: `Awareness`

```ts
class AssessCharacterAction extends PowerActionBase {
  constructor() {
    super(
      "assess_character",
      "Assess Character",
      1,
      "bonus",
      new SingleLivingEnemyRule(),
      new FixedManaCost(0),
      null,
      null
    );
  }

  prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction {
    const targetId = context.targetIds[0];
    return {
      actionId: this.id,
      powerId: "awareness",
      manaCost: this.cost.getManaCost(powerLevel, context),
      effects: [
        {
          kind: "intel_snapshot",
          payload: {
            casterId: context.casterId,
            targetId,
            level: powerLevel,
          },
        },
      ],
      activityLog: [`Assess Character: ${context.casterId} read ${targetId}.`],
      historyEntries: [
        {
          kind: "intel_snapshot",
          ownerId: context.casterId,
          targetId,
          level: powerLevel,
        },
      ],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

class AlertedSelfPassive extends PassiveFeatureBase {
  constructor() {
    super("alerted_self", "Alerted Self", 1);
  }

  apply(sheet: unknown, powerLevel: number): unknown {
    return sheet;
  }
}

export class AwarenessPower extends PowerBase {
  readonly id = "awareness" as const;
  readonly name = "Awareness";
  readonly abbreviation = "AW";
  readonly governingStat = "PER" as const;

  protected readonly actions = [new AssessCharacterAction()];
  protected readonly passives = [new AlertedSelfPassive()];
}
```

## Example subclass: `Healing`

```ts
class HealAction extends PowerActionBase {
  constructor() {
    super(
      "heal",
      "Heal",
      1,
      "standard",
      new MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, null, () => true),
      new FixedManaCost(2)
    );
  }

  prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction {
    return {
      actionId: this.id,
      powerId: "healing",
      manaCost: 2,
      effects: context.targetIds.map((targetId) => ({
        kind: "healing",
        payload: {
          targetId,
          amountFormula: { stat: "INT", bonus: powerLevel },
        },
      })),
      activityLog: [`Heal: ${context.casterId} affected ${context.targetIds.join(", ")}.`],
      historyEntries: [],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

class CureAction extends PowerActionBase {
  constructor() {
    super(
      "cure",
      "Cure",
      3,
      "standard",
      new MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, null, () => true),
      new FixedManaCost(3)
    );
  }

  prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction {
    return {
      actionId: this.id,
      powerId: "healing",
      manaCost: 3,
      effects: context.targetIds.map((targetId) => ({
        kind: "condition_removal",
        payload: {
          targetId,
          removes: ["poison", "disease", "curse"],
        },
      })),
      activityLog: [`Cure: ${context.casterId} affected ${context.targetIds.join(", ")}.`],
      historyEntries: [],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

export class HealingPower extends PowerBase {
  readonly id = "healing" as const;
  readonly name = "Healing";
  readonly abbreviation = "HL";
  readonly governingStat = "INT" as const;

  protected readonly actions = [
    new HealAction(),
    new CureAction(),
  ];
}
```

```ts
class LightAuraAction extends PowerActionBase {

    super(
      "light_aura",
      "Light Aura",
      1,
      "standard",

    );

    return {
      actionId: this.id,
      powerId: "light_support",

      effects: [
        {
          kind: "aura_source",

            casterId: context.casterId,
            allyBuff: true,
            enemyDebuff: powerLevel >= 5,
          },
        },
      ],
      activityLog: [`Light Aura: ${context.casterId} activated the aura.`],
      historyEntries: [],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

      historyEntries: [],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

  readonly name = "Light Support";

    new LightAuraAction(),
    new ManaRestoreAction(),
```

## Registry

```ts
export class PowerRegistry {
  private readonly powers = new Map<PowerId, PowerBase>();

  register(power: PowerBase): void {
    this.powers.set(power.id, power);
  }

  get(powerId: PowerId): PowerBase {
    const power = this.powers.get(powerId);
    if (!power) {
      throw new Error(`Unknown power: ${powerId}`);
    }
    return power;
  }

  list(): PowerBase[] {
    return [...this.powers.values()];
  }
}

export const powerRegistry = new PowerRegistry();
powerRegistry.register(new AwarenessPower());
powerRegistry.register(new HealingPower());
powerRegistry.register(new LightSupportPower());
```

## Why this is the right parent shape

Use inheritance for:
- `PowerBase`
- `PowerActionBase`
- `PassiveFeatureBase`

Use composition for:
- targeting
- costs
- upkeep
- usage limits
- aura/summon/damage/healing payload rules

That gives you:
- one stable parent contract
- easy new power creation
- easy new spell creation inside old or new powers
- fewer giant `switch` blocks
- less nullable junk in one mega-class

If you want the next step, the clean repo-aligned move is:
- keep `json_refs/powers.json` as authored rules data
- add these classes in a new domain layer such as:
  - `src/domain/powers/PowerBase.ts`
  - `src/domain/powers/PowerActionBase.ts`
  - `src/domain/powers/PowerRegistry.ts`
  - `src/domain/powers/definitions/*.ts`
- then gradually adapt [powerEffects.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerEffects.ts) and [combatEncounterCasting.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\lib\combatEncounterCasting.ts) to consume the registry instead of hardcoded branching.

### 638. Assistant

My design suggestion is a hybrid OOP + composition model:

- `PowerBase` = parent for every power
- `PowerActionBase` = parent for every castable spell/action under a power
- `PassiveFeatureBase` = parent for always-on, trigger-based, or derived features
- use composition for:
  - cost
  - targeting
  - usage limits
  - upkeep
  - aura behavior
  - summon behavior
  - damage/healing payloads

Why: one giant parent with 100 nullable fields will rot fast. A stable parent class should define lifecycle and contracts, while composition handles different mechanics.

This fits your current repo because today the logic is split across:
- [powerData.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerData.ts)
- [powerEffects.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerEffects.ts)
- [combatEncounterCasting.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\lib\combatEncounterCasting.ts)

I would evolve it toward this shape.

## Parent classes

```ts
export abstract class PowerActionBase implements PowerFeature {
  constructor(
    public readonly id: ActionId,
    public readonly label: string,
    public readonly introducedAtLevel: number,
    public readonly actionType: ActionType,
    public readonly targeting: TargetingRule,
    public readonly cost: CostRule,
    public readonly usage: UsageRule | null = null,
    public readonly upkeep: UpkeepRule | null = null
  ) {}

  isUnlocked(powerLevel: number): boolean {
    return powerLevel >= this.introducedAtLevel;
  }

  validate(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): ValidationResult {
    const errors: string[] = [];
    const warnings: string[] = [];

    if (!this.isUnlocked(powerLevel)) {
      errors.push(`${this.label} is not unlocked.`);
    }

    if (context.targetIds.length < this.targeting.minTargets) {
      errors.push(`Too few targets for ${this.label}.`);
    }

    if (
      this.targeting.maxTargets !== null &&
      context.targetIds.length > this.targeting.maxTargets
    ) {
      errors.push(`Too many targets for ${this.label}.`);
    }

    for (const targetId of context.targetIds) {
      if (!this.targeting.canTarget(context, targetId)) {
        errors.push(`Invalid target ${targetId} for ${this.label}.`);
      }
    }

    if (this.usage && !this.usage.canUse(powerLevel, context)) {
      errors.push(`${this.label} has no remaining uses.`);
    }

    return { ok: errors.length === 0, errors, warnings };
  }

  abstract prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction;
}

export abstract class PowerBase {
  abstract readonly id: PowerId;
  abstract readonly name: string;
  abstract readonly abbreviation: string;
  abstract readonly governingStat: GoverningStat;

  protected readonly actions: PowerActionBase[] = [];
  protected readonly passives: PassiveFeatureBase[] = [];

  getActions(powerLevel: number): PowerActionBase[] {
    return this.actions.filter((action) => action.isUnlocked(powerLevel));
  }

  getPassives(powerLevel: number): PassiveFeatureBase[] {
    return this.passives.filter((feature) => feature.isUnlocked(powerLevel));
  }

  getAction(actionId: string): PowerActionBase | undefined {
    return this.actions.find((action) => action.id === actionId);
  }

  describeLevel(powerLevel: number): string[] {
    const labels = [
      ...this.getActions(powerLevel).map((entry) => entry.label),
      ...this.getPassives(powerLevel).map((entry) => entry.label),
    ];
    return labels;
  }
}
```

## Reusable composition pieces

```ts
export class FixedManaCost implements CostRule {
  constructor(private readonly value: number) {}
  getManaCost(): number {
    return this.value;
  }
}

export class NoUsageLimit implements UsageRule {
  resetScope: ResetScope = "none";
  key = "none";
  canUse(): boolean {
    return true;
  }
  buildUsageChange(): Record<string, unknown>[] {
    return [];
  }
}

export class SelfTargetRule implements TargetingRule {
  mode: TargetMode = "self";
  minTargets = 1;
  maxTargets = 1;
  canTarget(context: CastContext, targetId: string): boolean {
    return context.casterId === targetId;
  }
}

export class SingleLivingEnemyRule implements TargetingRule {
  mode: TargetMode = "single";
  minTargets = 1;
  maxTargets = 1;
  canTarget(context: CastContext, targetId: string): boolean {
    return context.casterId !== targetId;
  }
}

export class MultiTargetRule implements TargetingRule {
  constructor(
    public readonly mode: TargetMode,
    public readonly minTargets: number,
    public readonly maxTargets: number | null,
    private readonly predicate: (context: CastContext, targetId: string) => boolean
  ) {}

  canTarget(context: CastContext, targetId: string): boolean {
    return this.predicate(context, targetId);
  }
}
```

## Example subclass: `Awareness`

```ts
class AssessCharacterAction extends PowerActionBase {
  constructor() {
    super(
      "assess_character",
      "Assess Character",
      1,
      "bonus",
      new SingleLivingEnemyRule(),
      new FixedManaCost(0),
      null,
      null
    );
  }

  prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction {
    const targetId = context.targetIds[0];
    return {
      actionId: this.id,
      powerId: "awareness",
      manaCost: this.cost.getManaCost(powerLevel, context),
      effects: [
        {
          kind: "intel_snapshot",
          payload: {
            casterId: context.casterId,
            targetId,
            level: powerLevel,
          },
        },
      ],
      activityLog: [`Assess Character: ${context.casterId} read ${targetId}.`],
      historyEntries: [
        {
          kind: "intel_snapshot",
          ownerId: context.casterId,
          targetId,
          level: powerLevel,
        },
      ],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

class AlertedSelfPassive extends PassiveFeatureBase {
  constructor() {
    super("alerted_self", "Alerted Self", 1);
  }

  apply(sheet: unknown, powerLevel: number): unknown {
    return sheet;
  }
}

export class AwarenessPower extends PowerBase {
  readonly id = "awareness" as const;
  readonly name = "Awareness";
  readonly abbreviation = "AW";
  readonly governingStat = "PER" as const;

  protected readonly actions = [new AssessCharacterAction()];
  protected readonly passives = [new AlertedSelfPassive()];
}
```

## Example subclass: `Healing`

```ts
class HealAction extends PowerActionBase {
  constructor() {
    super(
      "heal",
      "Heal",
      1,
      "standard",
      new MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, null, () => true),
      new FixedManaCost(2)
    );
  }

  prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction {
    return {
      actionId: this.id,
      powerId: "healing",
      manaCost: 2,
      effects: context.targetIds.map((targetId) => ({
        kind: "healing",
        payload: {
          targetId,
          amountFormula: { stat: "INT", bonus: powerLevel },
        },
      })),
      activityLog: [`Heal: ${context.casterId} affected ${context.targetIds.join(", ")}.`],
      historyEntries: [],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

class CureAction extends PowerActionBase {
  constructor() {
    super(
      "cure",
      "Cure",
      3,
      "standard",
      new MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, null, () => true),
      new FixedManaCost(3)
    );
  }

  prepare(powerLevel: number, context: CastContext): PreparedAction {
    return {
      actionId: this.id,
      powerId: "healing",
      manaCost: 3,
      effects: context.targetIds.map((targetId) => ({
        kind: "condition_removal",
        payload: {
          targetId,
          removes: ["poison", "disease", "curse"],
        },
      })),
      activityLog: [`Cure: ${context.casterId} affected ${context.targetIds.join(", ")}.`],
      historyEntries: [],
      usageChanges: [],
      summonChanges: [],
      ongoingStateChanges: [],
      resourceChanges: [],
      statusChanges: [],
    };
  }
}

export class HealingPower extends PowerBase {
  readonly id = "healing" as const;
  readonly name = "Healing";
  readonly abbreviation = "HL";
  readonly governingStat = "INT" as const;

  protected readonly actions = [
    new HealAction(),
    new CureAction(),
  ];
}
```

## Registry

```ts
export class PowerRegistry {
  private readonly powers = new Map<PowerId, PowerBase>();

  register(power: PowerBase): void {
    this.powers.set(power.id, power);
  }

  get(powerId: PowerId): PowerBase {
    const power = this.powers.get(powerId);
    if (!power) {
      throw new Error(`Unknown power: ${powerId}`);
    }
    return power;
  }

  list(): PowerBase[] {
    return [...this.powers.values()];
  }
}

export const powerRegistry = new PowerRegistry();
powerRegistry.register(new AwarenessPower());
powerRegistry.register(new HealingPower());
powerRegistry.register(new LightSupportPower());
```

## Why this is the right parent shape

Use inheritance for:
- `PowerBase`
- `PowerActionBase`
- `PassiveFeatureBase`

Use composition for:
- targeting
- costs
- upkeep
- usage limits
- aura/summon/damage/healing payload rules

That gives you:
- one stable parent contract
- easy new power creation
- easy new spell creation inside old or new powers
- fewer giant `switch` blocks
- less nullable junk in one mega-class

If you want the next step, the clean repo-aligned move is:
- keep `json_refs/powers.json` as authored rules data
- add these classes in a new domain layer such as:
  - `src/domain/powers/PowerBase.ts`
  - `src/domain/powers/PowerActionBase.ts`
  - `src/domain/powers/PowerRegistry.ts`
  - `src/domain/powers/definitions/*.ts`
- then gradually adapt [powerEffects.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerEffects.ts) and [combatEncounterCasting.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\lib\combatEncounterCasting.ts) to consume the registry instead of hardcoded branching.

### 640. Assistant

1. No. Our current structure is not like that.

2. Current repo structure is closer to this:

- `PowerEntry` on the character sheet is just data:
  - `id`
  - `name`
  - `level`
  - `governingStat`
- power rule definitions live in JSON:
  - [powers.json](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\json_refs\powers.json)
- those JSON rules are loaded by lookup helpers:
  - [powerData.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerData.ts)
- cast options / variants / target modes / mana logic are mostly function-based:
  - [powerEffects.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerEffects.ts)
- encounter casting orchestration is also function-based:
  - [combatEncounterCasting.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\lib\combatEncounterCasting.ts)
- summon logic is split separately:
  - [summons.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\summons.ts)

So today it is:
- data-driven
- functional
- rule lookup + big helper functions

Not:
- `Power` objects with methods
- `Spell` subclasses
- a clean parent `PowerBase` / `SpellBase` hierarchy

3. Yes. Here is the Python equivalent of the design I suggested.

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Literal, Optional, Any


PowerId = Literal[
    "awareness",
    "body_reinforcement",
    "crowd_control",
    "elementalist",
    "healing",
    "light_support",
    "necromancy",
    "shadow_control",
]

GoverningStat = Literal["STR", "DEX", "STAM", "CHA", "APP", "MAN", "INT", "WITS", "PER"]
ActionType = Literal["free", "bonus", "standard", "reaction", "passive"]
TargetMode = Literal["self", "single", "multiple", "party", "encounter", "none"]
ResetScope = Literal["daily", "longRest", "perTargetDaily", "encounter", "none"]


@dataclass
class CastContext:
    caster_id: str
    target_ids: list[str]
    encounter_id: Optional[str] = None
    now_iso: str = ""
    source: Literal["sheet", "encounter"] = "encounter"
    items_by_id: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    read_character: Any = None
    random: Any = None


@dataclass
class ValidationResult:
    ok: bool
    errors: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    warnings: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)


@dataclass
class PreparedEffect:
    kind: str
    payload: dict[str, Any]


@dataclass
class PreparedAction:
    action_id: str
    power_id: PowerId
    mana_cost: int
    effects: list[PreparedEffect] = field(default_factory=list)
    activity_log: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    history_entries: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    usage_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    summon_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    ongoing_state_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    resource_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    status_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)


class TargetingRule(ABC):
    mode: TargetMode
    min_targets: int
    max_targets: Optional[int]

    @abstractmethod
    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        pass


class CostRule(ABC):
    @abstractmethod
    def get_mana_cost(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> int:
        pass


class UsageRule(ABC):
    reset_scope: ResetScope
    key: str

    @abstractmethod
    def can_use(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> bool:
        pass

    @abstractmethod
    def build_usage_change(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        pass


class UpkeepRule(ABC):
    enabled: bool

    @abstractmethod
    def get_upkeep_cost(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> int:
        pass

    @abstractmethod
    def build_ongoing_state(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
        pass


class PowerFeature(ABC):
    id: str
    label: str
    introduced_at_level: int

    @abstractmethod
    def is_unlocked(self, power_level: int) -> bool:
        pass


class PassiveFeatureBase(PowerFeature, ABC):
    def __init__(self, feature_id: str, label: str, introduced_at_level: int):
        self.id = feature_id
        self.label = label
        self.introduced_at_level = introduced_at_level

    def is_unlocked(self, power_level: int) -> bool:
        return power_level >= self.introduced_at_level

    @abstractmethod
    def apply(self, sheet: Any, power_level: int, context: Any = None) -> Any:
        pass


class PowerActionBase(PowerFeature, ABC):
    def __init__(
        self,
        action_id: str,
        label: str,
        introduced_at_level: int,
        action_type: ActionType,
        targeting: TargetingRule,
        cost: CostRule,
        usage: Optional[UsageRule] = None,
        upkeep: Optional[UpkeepRule] = None,
    ):
        self.id = action_id
        self.label = label
        self.introduced_at_level = introduced_at_level
        self.action_type = action_type
        self.targeting = targeting
        self.cost = cost
        self.usage = usage
        self.upkeep = upkeep

    def is_unlocked(self, power_level: int) -> bool:
        return power_level >= self.introduced_at_level

    def validate(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> ValidationResult:
        errors: list[str] = []
        warnings: list[str] = []

        if not self.is_unlocked(power_level):
            errors.append(f"{self.label} is not unlocked.")

        if len(context.target_ids) < self.targeting.min_targets:
            errors.append(f"Too few targets for {self.label}.")

        if self.targeting.max_targets is not None and len(context.target_ids) > self.targeting.max_targets:
            errors.append(f"Too many targets for {self.label}.")

        for target_id in context.target_ids:
            if not self.targeting.can_target(context, target_id):
                errors.append(f"Invalid target {target_id} for {self.label}.")

        if self.usage and not self.usage.can_use(power_level, context):
            errors.append(f"{self.label} has no remaining uses.")

        return ValidationResult(ok=(len(errors) == 0), errors=errors, warnings=warnings)

    @abstractmethod
    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        pass


class PowerBase(ABC):
    id: PowerId
    name: str
    abbreviation: str
    governing_stat: GoverningStat

    def __init__(self):
        self.actions: list[PowerActionBase] = []
        self.passives: list[PassiveFeatureBase] = []

    def get_actions(self, power_level: int) -> list[PowerActionBase]:
        return [action for action in self.actions if action.is_unlocked(power_level)]

    def get_passives(self, power_level: int) -> list[PassiveFeatureBase]:
        return [feature for feature in self.passives if feature.is_unlocked(power_level)]

    def get_action(self, action_id: str) -> Optional[PowerActionBase]:
        for action in self.actions:
            if action.id == action_id:
                return action
        return None

    def describe_level(self, power_level: int) -> list[str]:
        labels = [action.label for action in self.get_actions(power_level)]
        labels += [feature.label for feature in self.get_passives(power_level)]
        return labels


class FixedManaCost(CostRule):
    def __init__(self, value: int):
        self.value = value

    def get_mana_cost(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> int:
        return self.value


class NoUsageLimit(UsageRule):
    reset_scope: ResetScope = "none"
    key = "none"

    def can_use(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> bool:
        return True

    def build_usage_change(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        return []


class SelfTargetRule(TargetingRule):
    mode: TargetMode = "self"
    min_targets = 1
    max_targets = 1

    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        return context.caster_id == target_id


class SingleOtherTargetRule(TargetingRule):
    mode: TargetMode = "single"
    min_targets = 1
    max_targets = 1

    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        return context.caster_id != target_id


class MultiTargetRule(TargetingRule):
    def __init__(
        self,
        mode: TargetMode,
        min_targets: int,
        max_targets: Optional[int],
        predicate: Any,
    ):
        self.mode = mode
        self.min_targets = min_targets
        self.max_targets = max_targets
        self.predicate = predicate

    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        return self.predicate(context, target_id)


class AssessCharacterAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="assess_character",
            label="Assess Character",
            introduced_at_level=1,
            action_type="bonus",
            targeting=SingleOtherTargetRule(),
            cost=FixedManaCost(0),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        target_id = context.target_ids[0]
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="awareness",
            mana_cost=self.cost.get_mana_cost(power_level, context),
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="intel_snapshot",
                    payload={
                        "caster_id": context.caster_id,
                        "target_id": target_id,
                        "level": power_level,
                    },
                )
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Assess Character: {context.caster_id} read {target_id}."],
            history_entries=[
                {
                    "kind": "intel_snapshot",
                    "owner_id": context.caster_id,
                    "target_id": target_id,
                    "level": power_level,
                }
            ],
        )


class AlertedSelfPassive(PassiveFeatureBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__("alerted_self", "Alerted Self", 1)

    def apply(self, sheet: Any, power_level: int, context: Any = None) -> Any:
        return sheet


class AwarenessPower(PowerBase):
    id: PowerId = "awareness"
    name = "Awareness"
    abbreviation = "AW"
    governing_stat: GoverningStat = "PER"

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.actions = [AssessCharacterAction()]
        self.passives = [AlertedSelfPassive()]


class HealAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="heal",
            label="Heal",
            introduced_at_level=1,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, None, lambda context, target_id: True),
            cost=FixedManaCost(2),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="healing",
            mana_cost=2,
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="healing",
                    payload={
                        "target_id": target_id,
                        "amount_formula": {"stat": "INT", "bonus": power_level},
                    },
                )
                for target_id in context.target_ids
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Heal: {context.caster_id} affected {', '.join(context.target_ids)}."],
        )


class CureAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="cure",
            label="Cure",
            introduced_at_level=3,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, None, lambda context, target_id: True),
            cost=FixedManaCost(3),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="healing",
            mana_cost=3,
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="condition_removal",
                    payload={
                        "target_id": target_id,
                        "removes": ["poison", "disease", "curse"],
                    },
                )
                for target_id in context.target_ids
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Cure: {context.caster_id} affected {', '.join(context.target_ids)}."],
        )


class HealingPower(PowerBase):
    id: PowerId = "healing"
    name = "Healing"
    abbreviation = "HL"
    governing_stat: GoverningStat = "INT"

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.actions = [HealAction(), CureAction()]

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="light_aura",
            label="Light Aura",
            introduced_at_level=1,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=SelfTargetRule(),
            cost=FixedManaCost(2),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="light_support",
            mana_cost=self.cost.get_mana_cost(power_level, context),
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="aura_source",
                    payload={
                        "caster_id": context.caster_id,
                        "ally_buff": True,

                    },
                )
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Light Aura: {context.caster_id} activated the aura."],

class ManaRestoreAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="mana_restore",
            label="Mana Restore",
            introduced_at_level=4,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=SingleOtherTargetRule(),
            cost=FixedManaCost(0),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="light_support",
            mana_cost=0,
            activity_log=[f"Mana Restore: {context.caster_id} restored mana."],
        )


class LightSupportPower(PowerBase):
    id: PowerId = "light_support"
    name = "Light Support"
    abbreviation = "LS"
    governing_stat: GoverningStat = "APP"

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.actions = [LightAuraAction(), ManaRestoreAction()]


class PowerRegistry:
    def __init__(self):
        self._powers: dict[PowerId, PowerBase] = {}

    def register(self, power: PowerBase) -> None:
        self._powers[power.id] = power

    def get(self, power_id: PowerId) -> PowerBase:
        if power_id not in self._powers:
            raise KeyError(f"Unknown power: {power_id}")
        return self._powers[power_id]

    def list(self) -> list[PowerBase]:
        return list(self._powers.values())


power_registry = PowerRegistry()
power_registry.register(AwarenessPower())
power_registry.register(HealingPower())
power_registry.register(LightSupportPower())
```

Short version:
- current repo: data + functions
- suggested design: classes for powers/actions, composition for mechanics
- Python above is the direct equivalent of that suggested design

Also, I identified another unfinished item from your question and added it to TODO:
- power/spell OOP domain model design is not implemented in the repo today

### 641. Assistant

1. No. Our current structure is not like that.

2. Current repo structure is closer to this:

- `PowerEntry` on the character sheet is just data:
  - `id`
  - `name`
  - `level`
  - `governingStat`
- power rule definitions live in JSON:
  - [powers.json](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\json_refs\powers.json)
- those JSON rules are loaded by lookup helpers:
  - [powerData.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerData.ts)
- cast options / variants / target modes / mana logic are mostly function-based:
  - [powerEffects.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\powerEffects.ts)
- encounter casting orchestration is also function-based:
  - [combatEncounterCasting.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\lib\combatEncounterCasting.ts)
- summon logic is split separately:
  - [summons.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\summons.ts)

So today it is:
- data-driven
- functional
- rule lookup + big helper functions

Not:
- `Power` objects with methods
- `Spell` subclasses
- a clean parent `PowerBase` / `SpellBase` hierarchy

3. Yes. Here is the Python equivalent of the design I suggested.

```python
from __future__ import annotations

from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Literal, Optional, Any


PowerId = Literal[
    "awareness",
    "body_reinforcement",
    "crowd_control",
    "elementalist",
    "healing",
    "light_support",
    "necromancy",
    "shadow_control",
]

GoverningStat = Literal["STR", "DEX", "STAM", "CHA", "APP", "MAN", "INT", "WITS", "PER"]
ActionType = Literal["free", "bonus", "standard", "reaction", "passive"]
TargetMode = Literal["self", "single", "multiple", "party", "encounter", "none"]
ResetScope = Literal["daily", "longRest", "perTargetDaily", "encounter", "none"]


@dataclass
class CastContext:
    caster_id: str
    target_ids: list[str]
    encounter_id: Optional[str] = None
    now_iso: str = ""
    source: Literal["sheet", "encounter"] = "encounter"
    items_by_id: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    read_character: Any = None
    random: Any = None


@dataclass
class ValidationResult:
    ok: bool
    errors: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    warnings: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)


@dataclass
class PreparedEffect:
    kind: str
    payload: dict[str, Any]


@dataclass
class PreparedAction:
    action_id: str
    power_id: PowerId
    mana_cost: int
    effects: list[PreparedEffect] = field(default_factory=list)
    activity_log: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    history_entries: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    usage_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    summon_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    ongoing_state_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    resource_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
    status_changes: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)


class TargetingRule(ABC):
    mode: TargetMode
    min_targets: int
    max_targets: Optional[int]

    @abstractmethod
    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        pass


class CostRule(ABC):
    @abstractmethod
    def get_mana_cost(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> int:
        pass


class UsageRule(ABC):
    reset_scope: ResetScope
    key: str

    @abstractmethod
    def can_use(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> bool:
        pass

    @abstractmethod
    def build_usage_change(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        pass


class UpkeepRule(ABC):
    enabled: bool

    @abstractmethod
    def get_upkeep_cost(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> int:
        pass

    @abstractmethod
    def build_ongoing_state(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> Optional[dict[str, Any]]:
        pass


class PowerFeature(ABC):
    id: str
    label: str
    introduced_at_level: int

    @abstractmethod
    def is_unlocked(self, power_level: int) -> bool:
        pass


class PassiveFeatureBase(PowerFeature, ABC):
    def __init__(self, feature_id: str, label: str, introduced_at_level: int):
        self.id = feature_id
        self.label = label
        self.introduced_at_level = introduced_at_level

    def is_unlocked(self, power_level: int) -> bool:
        return power_level >= self.introduced_at_level

    @abstractmethod
    def apply(self, sheet: Any, power_level: int, context: Any = None) -> Any:
        pass


class PowerActionBase(PowerFeature, ABC):
    def __init__(
        self,
        action_id: str,
        label: str,
        introduced_at_level: int,
        action_type: ActionType,
        targeting: TargetingRule,
        cost: CostRule,
        usage: Optional[UsageRule] = None,
        upkeep: Optional[UpkeepRule] = None,
    ):
        self.id = action_id
        self.label = label
        self.introduced_at_level = introduced_at_level
        self.action_type = action_type
        self.targeting = targeting
        self.cost = cost
        self.usage = usage
        self.upkeep = upkeep

    def is_unlocked(self, power_level: int) -> bool:
        return power_level >= self.introduced_at_level

    def validate(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> ValidationResult:
        errors: list[str] = []
        warnings: list[str] = []

        if not self.is_unlocked(power_level):
            errors.append(f"{self.label} is not unlocked.")

        if len(context.target_ids) < self.targeting.min_targets:
            errors.append(f"Too few targets for {self.label}.")

        if self.targeting.max_targets is not None and len(context.target_ids) > self.targeting.max_targets:
            errors.append(f"Too many targets for {self.label}.")

        for target_id in context.target_ids:
            if not self.targeting.can_target(context, target_id):
                errors.append(f"Invalid target {target_id} for {self.label}.")

        if self.usage and not self.usage.can_use(power_level, context):
            errors.append(f"{self.label} has no remaining uses.")

        return ValidationResult(ok=(len(errors) == 0), errors=errors, warnings=warnings)

    @abstractmethod
    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        pass


class PowerBase(ABC):
    id: PowerId
    name: str
    abbreviation: str
    governing_stat: GoverningStat

    def __init__(self):
        self.actions: list[PowerActionBase] = []
        self.passives: list[PassiveFeatureBase] = []

    def get_actions(self, power_level: int) -> list[PowerActionBase]:
        return [action for action in self.actions if action.is_unlocked(power_level)]

    def get_passives(self, power_level: int) -> list[PassiveFeatureBase]:
        return [feature for feature in self.passives if feature.is_unlocked(power_level)]

    def get_action(self, action_id: str) -> Optional[PowerActionBase]:
        for action in self.actions:
            if action.id == action_id:
                return action
        return None

    def describe_level(self, power_level: int) -> list[str]:
        labels = [action.label for action in self.get_actions(power_level)]
        labels += [feature.label for feature in self.get_passives(power_level)]
        return labels


class FixedManaCost(CostRule):
    def __init__(self, value: int):
        self.value = value

    def get_mana_cost(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> int:
        return self.value


class NoUsageLimit(UsageRule):
    reset_scope: ResetScope = "none"
    key = "none"

    def can_use(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> bool:
        return True

    def build_usage_change(self, level: int, context: CastContext) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        return []


class SelfTargetRule(TargetingRule):
    mode: TargetMode = "self"
    min_targets = 1
    max_targets = 1

    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        return context.caster_id == target_id


class SingleOtherTargetRule(TargetingRule):
    mode: TargetMode = "single"
    min_targets = 1
    max_targets = 1

    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        return context.caster_id != target_id


class MultiTargetRule(TargetingRule):
    def __init__(
        self,
        mode: TargetMode,
        min_targets: int,
        max_targets: Optional[int],
        predicate: Any,
    ):
        self.mode = mode
        self.min_targets = min_targets
        self.max_targets = max_targets
        self.predicate = predicate

    def can_target(self, context: CastContext, target_id: str) -> bool:
        return self.predicate(context, target_id)


class AssessCharacterAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="assess_character",
            label="Assess Character",
            introduced_at_level=1,
            action_type="bonus",
            targeting=SingleOtherTargetRule(),
            cost=FixedManaCost(0),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        target_id = context.target_ids[0]
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="awareness",
            mana_cost=self.cost.get_mana_cost(power_level, context),
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="intel_snapshot",
                    payload={
                        "caster_id": context.caster_id,
                        "target_id": target_id,
                        "level": power_level,
                    },
                )
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Assess Character: {context.caster_id} read {target_id}."],
            history_entries=[
                {
                    "kind": "intel_snapshot",
                    "owner_id": context.caster_id,
                    "target_id": target_id,
                    "level": power_level,
                }
            ],
        )


class AlertedSelfPassive(PassiveFeatureBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__("alerted_self", "Alerted Self", 1)

    def apply(self, sheet: Any, power_level: int, context: Any = None) -> Any:
        return sheet


class AwarenessPower(PowerBase):
    id: PowerId = "awareness"
    name = "Awareness"
    abbreviation = "AW"
    governing_stat: GoverningStat = "PER"

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.actions = [AssessCharacterAction()]
        self.passives = [AlertedSelfPassive()]


class HealAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="heal",
            label="Heal",
            introduced_at_level=1,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, None, lambda context, target_id: True),
            cost=FixedManaCost(2),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="healing",
            mana_cost=2,
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="healing",
                    payload={
                        "target_id": target_id,
                        "amount_formula": {"stat": "INT", "bonus": power_level},
                    },
                )
                for target_id in context.target_ids
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Heal: {context.caster_id} affected {', '.join(context.target_ids)}."],
        )


class CureAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="cure",
            label="Cure",
            introduced_at_level=3,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=MultiTargetRule("multiple", 1, None, lambda context, target_id: True),
            cost=FixedManaCost(3),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="healing",
            mana_cost=3,
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="condition_removal",
                    payload={
                        "target_id": target_id,
                        "removes": ["poison", "disease", "curse"],
                    },
                )
                for target_id in context.target_ids
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Cure: {context.caster_id} affected {', '.join(context.target_ids)}."],
        )


class HealingPower(PowerBase):
    id: PowerId = "healing"
    name = "Healing"
    abbreviation = "HL"
    governing_stat: GoverningStat = "INT"

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.actions = [HealAction(), CureAction()]


class LightAuraAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="light_aura",
            label="Light Aura",
            introduced_at_level=1,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=SelfTargetRule(),
            cost=FixedManaCost(2),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="light_support",
            mana_cost=self.cost.get_mana_cost(power_level, context),
            effects=[
                PreparedEffect(
                    kind="aura_source",
                    payload={
                        "caster_id": context.caster_id,
                        "ally_buff": True,
                        "enemy_debuff": power_level >= 5,
                    },
                )
            ],
            activity_log=[f"Light Aura: {context.caster_id} activated the aura."],
        )


class ManaRestoreAction(PowerActionBase):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__(
            action_id="mana_restore",
            label="Mana Restore",
            introduced_at_level=4,
            action_type="standard",
            targeting=SingleOtherTargetRule(),
            cost=FixedManaCost(0),
        )

    def prepare(self, power_level: int, context: CastContext) -> PreparedAction:
        return PreparedAction(
            action_id=self.id,
            power_id="light_support",
            mana_cost=0,
            activity_log=[f"Mana Restore: {context.caster_id} restored mana."],
        )


class LightSupportPower(PowerBase):
    id: PowerId = "light_support"
    name = "Light Support"
    abbreviation = "LS"
    governing_stat: GoverningStat = "APP"

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.actions = [LightAuraAction(), ManaRestoreAction()]


class PowerRegistry:
    def __init__(self):
        self._powers: dict[PowerId, PowerBase] = {}

    def register(self, power: PowerBase) -> None:
        self._powers[power.id] = power

    def get(self, power_id: PowerId) -> PowerBase:
        if power_id not in self._powers:
            raise KeyError(f"Unknown power: {power_id}")
        return self._powers[power_id]

    def list(self) -> list[PowerBase]:
        return list(self._powers.values())


power_registry = PowerRegistry()
power_registry.register(AwarenessPower())
power_registry.register(HealingPower())
power_registry.register(LightSupportPower())
```

- current repo: data + functions

- Python above is the direct equivalent of that suggested design

**2. ARCHITECTURE**

- File/folder structure (relevant parts only)
  - `src/routes/`

  - `project_tracking/`

- Data models / schemas
  - `CharacterDraft` in [characterTemplate.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\config\characterTemplate.ts)
    - stats, skills, powers, `activePowerEffects`, `powerUsageState`, shared item refs, status tags, game history
  - `CombatEncounterState` in [combatEncounter.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\types\combatEncounter.ts)
    - parties, participants, turn state, transient summons, ongoing states, activity log
  - `PreparedCastRequest` in [combatEncounterView.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\types\combatEncounterView.ts)
    - unified payload for cast/attack/special execution
  - Shared item model in [items.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\types\items.ts)
    - standalone item records; character sheets store refs, not embedded items
- Key design decisions
  - Power system is currently data-driven + function-based, not OOP class-based.
  - `powers.json` + `powerData.ts` provide runtime power definitions.
  - Encounter actions normalize into `PreparedCastRequest`, then route execution mutates sheet/encounter state.
  - `Expose Darkness` is not separate anymore; it is the enemy-side of Light Aura Lv5.
  - `Body Reinforcement` revive is manual in encounter, not auto on turn advance.
  - Physical attacks are loadout-driven and auto-resolve from equipped hand slots.

**3. CURRENT IMPLEMENTATION**
- Main components/modules

  - [buildCharacterEncounterSnapshot](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\rules\combatEncounter.ts)
    - encounter-visible derived snapshot
  - [buildCharacterDerivedValues](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\config\characterRuntime.ts)
    - derived stats, resources, passives, utility traits
- Important flows (step-by-step)
  - Power cast
    - select power/variant/targets in cast form
    - `prepareCastRequest(...)`
    - optional confirmation
    - `executePreparedCast(...)`
    - apply mana/effects/healing/damage/status/history/activity log
  - Physical attack
    - select target only
    - resolve profile from equipped hands/items
    - auto-roll hit pool
    - compare vs target AC
    - marginal added to damage pool
    - auto-roll damage pool
    - subtract DR
    - apply damage + activity log
  - BR manual revive
    - power controls compute `getBodyReinforcementReviveState`
    - if BR >= 2 and HP in `0..-5` and daily use unspent, button is enabled
    - trigger builds `PreparedCastRequest`
    - execution sets HP to `1` or `4`, increments daily use, writes activity log
  - Assess Character
    - action resolves in encounter
    - full intel snapshot is saved into caster’s `gameHistory`
    - encounter activity log gets short line
    - current character sheet renderer only shows short summary, not full snapshot details

**4. STATE OF REFACTORING**
- What has been refactored
  - Encounter UI split into smaller components.
  - Shared libs/selectors/view-models introduced.
  - Shared item model extracted from embedded character items.
  - `Derived Summary` consolidated.
  - Physical attacks moved to dedicated helper.
  - BR manual special action moved to dedicated helper.
- What remains
  - `CombatEncounterPage.tsx` still owns too much orchestration.
  - `CharacterHistorySection.tsx` does not render full intel snapshots.
  - Full item authoring / AA sharing UI deferred.
- Known technical debt
  - Route-heavy encounter execution (`ARCH-REM-01`).
  - Power system is still large function-switch logic, not modular per-power objects.
  - Some docs/tracking are very history-heavy and may need pruning later.
  - `CS-UI-02` validated but not committed; workspace dirty.

  - Use `apply_patch` for edits.
  - Keep changes minimal/coherent.
  - Prefer ASCII.
  - Keep tracking current.
- Constraints to respect
  - `references/plan.md` is authoritative.
  - Start with earliest unfinished actionable item.
  - Do not mark done until `npm run typecheck`, `npm test`, `npm run build` all pass.
  - If a pre-existing failure appears, log/isolate it first.
  - Add newly identified unfinished work to TODO immediately.
- “Do not break” parts
  - Negative HP support.
  - AC intel snapshots belong in caster’s `gameHistory`.
  - Light Aura Lv5 integrated enemy debuff behavior.
  - Crowd Control auto-contest and single visible tag.
  - BR manual trigger behavior.
  - Automatic physical attacks:
    - no weapon => brawl/fists
    - equipped `brawl` item => brawl profile
    - bow occupies both hands
    - single-target UI for now

  - Do not break completed Phase 1 combat behavior.

**2. ARCHITECTURE**
- Tech stack
  - React + TypeScript + Vite
  - Local persistence only
  - Node-based custom test harness (`tests/run-tests.ts`)
- File/folder structure (relevant parts only)
  - `src/routes/`
    - [CombatEncounterPage.tsx](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\routes\CombatEncounterPage.tsx)
    - [PlayerCharacterPage.tsx](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\routes\PlayerCharacterPage.tsx)
  - `src/components/combat-encounter/`
    - combat UI/forms/cards/panels
  - `src/components/player-character/`
    - character sheet sections
  - `src/lib/`
    - orchestration helpers, ids, power usage, item helpers, physical/special action helpers
  - `src/rules/`
    - power rules, combat resolution, encounter snapshot rules, summon rules, runtime power data
  - `src/config/`
    - character template/runtime derivation
  - `src/types/`
    - encounter, view, item, power-usage types
  - `json_refs/`
    - [powers.json](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\json_refs\powers.json)
  - `project_tracking/`
    - live TODO/done/log
  - `references/`
    - plan, notes, objective, rule references
- Data models / schemas
  - `CharacterDraft` in [characterTemplate.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\config\characterTemplate.ts)
    - stats, skills, powers, `activePowerEffects`, `powerUsageState`, shared item refs, status tags, game history
  - `CombatEncounterState` in [combatEncounter.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\types\combatEncounter.ts)
    - parties, participants, turn state, transient summons, ongoing states, activity log
  - `PreparedCastRequest` in [combatEncounterView.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\types\combatEncounterView.ts)
    - unified payload for cast/attack/special execution
  - Shared item model in [items.ts](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\types\items.ts)
    - standalone item records; character sheets store refs, not embedded items
- Key design decisions
  - Power system is currently data-driven + function-based, not OOP class-based.
  - `powers.json` + `powerData.ts` provide runtime power definitions.
  - Encounter actions normalize into `PreparedCastRequest`, then route execution mutates sheet/encounter state.
  - `Expose Darkness` is not separate anymore; it is the enemy-side of Light Aura Lv5.
  - `Body Reinforcement` revive is manual in encounter, not auto on turn advance.
  - Physical attacks are loadout-driven and auto-resolve from equipped hand slots.

**3. CURRENT IMPLEMENTATION**
- Main components/modules
  - [CombatEncounterPage.tsx](C:\Users\Evrim\Desktop\FRP\Convergence\game_hub5\src\routes\CombatEncounterPage.tsx)
